[?2004l#!/bin/bash
#This script will create a tmux session to tail all the process log files
#Started by Riley C on 9/20/2023
echo "To switch between windows use CTRL-B <WINDOW #>"
echo "To disconnect use CTRL-B d, NOT CTRL-D"
sleep 2
tmux new-session -d -s winlinkauto
tmux new-window -d -n pat -t winlinkauto:1 "bash"
tmux new-window -d -n rigctl -t winlinkauto:2 "bash"
tmux new-window -d -n ardop -t winlinkauto:3 "bash"
tmux new-window -d -n direwolf -t winlinkauto:4 "bash"
tmux new-window -d -n shell -t winlinkauto:5 "bash"
tmux send -t winlinkauto:1 "tail -f /var/log/winlinkauto/pat.log" C-m
tmux send -t winlinkauto:2 "tail -f /var/log/winlinkauto/rigctl.log" C-m
tmux send -t winlinkauto:3 "tail -f /var/log/winlinkauto/ardop.log" C-m
tmux send -t winlinkauto:4 "tail -f /var/log/winlinkauto/direwolf.log" C-m

tmux attach -t winlinkauto

Description=Direwolf for Winlinkauto
After=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=riley
Group=winlinkauto
ExecStart=bash -c "/usr/bin/direwolf -c /usr/local/etc/winlinkauto/direwolf.conf"
ExecStop=bash -c "killall direwolf"
StandardOutput=file:/var/log/winlinkauto/direwolf.log
StandardError=file:/var/log/winlinkauto/direwolf.log
Restart=always

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target

[?2004h]0;riley@hamey: ~/git/winlinkauto[01;32mriley@hamey[00m:[01;34m~/git/winlinkauto[00m$ cat [7mfind-gws.sh[27mfind-gws.sh
[?2004l#!/bin/bash
#This script will automatically send a message and try to connect to GW's on the chosen band
#Started by Riley C on 9/23
if [[ -z $1 ]] 
then
	echo "Enter the band you wish to test: "
	read band
else
	band=$1
fi
trap '{ echo "Hey, you pressed Ctrl-C.  Time to quit."; cleanup; exit 1; }' INT

gwldir="gwlists"
cfgdir="conf"
logdir="logs"
mycall=`pat env | grep MYCALL | awk -F "\"" '{print $2}'`
patmailbox=`pat env | grep MAILBOX | awk -F"\"" '{print $2}'`
outboxnum=`ls -ltr ${patmailbox}/${mycall}/out | grep -v total | wc -l`

cleanup() {
    rm ${patmailbox}/${mycall}/out/*
}



for run in 1 2 3 
do
	echo "###########################################################################"
	echo "Posting then sending message $run"
	echo "###########################################################################"
 	./pat-sender.sh n "Find GWs ${band} $run" "Testing sending  on ${band}.  Sent from `pwd`${0}, on `hostname`, at `date`. Message number $run." "riley@netandnix.net rec7788@hotmail.com"
 	./pat-connect-hf.sh $band 2 sggw
	echo "###########################################################################"
	echo "Taking a little break"
	echo "###########################################################################"
	sleep 120

done
cleanup

Usage:
  /usr/bin/pat-winlink [options] command [arguments]

Commands:
  connect         Connect to a remote station.
  interactive     Run interactive mode.
  http            Run http server for web UI.
  compose         Compose a new message.
  read            Read messages.
  composeform     Post form-based report.
  position        Post a position report (GPSd or manual entry).

  configure       Open configuration file for editing.
  version         Print the application version.
  env             List environment variables.

      --config string      Path to config file. (default "/home/riley/.config/pat/config.json")

Usage:
  /usr/bin/pat [options] command [arguments]

Commands:
  connect         Connect to a remote station.
  interactive     Run interactive mode.
  http            Run http server for web UI.
  compose         Compose a new message.
  read            Read messages.
  composeform     Post form-based report.

  configure       Open configuration file for editing.
  version         Print the application version.
  env             List environment variables.
  help            Print detailed help for a given command.

Options:
      --config string      Path to config file. (default "/home/riley/.config/pat/config.json")
      --event-log string   Path to event log file. (default "/home/riley/.local/state/pat/eventlog.json")
      --forms string       Path to forms directory. (default "/home/riley/.local/share/pat/Standard_Forms")
      --ignore-busy        Don't wait for clear channel before connecting to a node.
  -l, --listen string      Comma-separated list of methods to listen on (e.g. ardop,telnet,ax25).
      --log string         Path to log file. The file is truncated on each startup. (default "/home/riley/.local/state/pat/pat.log")
      --mbox string        Path to mailbox directory. (default "/home/riley/.local/share/pat/mailbox")
      --mycall string      Your callsign (winlink user).
      --radio-only         Radio Only mode (Winlink Hybrid RMS only).
  -s, --send-only          Download inbound messages later, send only.

Usage:
